class \+\_\+\+\_\+gnu\+\_\+pbds\+::detail\+::\+PB\+\_\+\+DS\+\_\+\+CC\+\_\+\+HASH\+\_\+\+NAME$<$ Key, Mapped, Hash\+\_\+\+Fn, Eq\+\_\+\+Fn, \+\_\+\+Alloc, Store\+\_\+\+Hash, Comb\+\_\+\+Hash\+\_\+\+Fn, Resize\+\_\+\+Policy $>$}
A collision-\/chaining hash-\/based container.


\begin{DoxyTemplParams}{Template Parameters}
{\em Key} & Key type.\\
\hline
{\em Mapped} & Map type.\\
\hline
{\em Hash\+\_\+\+Fn} & Hashing functor. Default is \+\_\+\+\_\+gnu\+\_\+cxx\+::hash.\\
\hline
{\em Eq\+\_\+\+Fn} & Equal functor. Default std\+::equal\+\_\+to$<$\+Key$>$\\
\hline
{\em \+\_\+\+Alloc} & Allocator type.\\
\hline
{\em Store\+\_\+\+Hash} & If key type stores extra metadata. Defaults to false.\\
\hline
{\em Comb\+\_\+\+Hash\+\_\+\+Fn} & Combining hash functor. If Hash\+\_\+\+Fn is not \doxylink{struct____gnu__pbds_1_1null__type}{null\+\_\+type}, then this is the ranged-\/hash functor; otherwise, this is the range-\/hashing functor. XXX(See Design\+::\+Hash-\/Based Containers\+::\+Hash Policies.) Default \doxylink{class____gnu__pbds_1_1direct__mask__range__hashing}{direct\+\_\+mask\+\_\+range\+\_\+hashing}.\\
\hline
{\em Resize\+\_\+\+Policy} & Resizes hash. Defaults to \doxylink{class____gnu__pbds_1_1hash__standard__resize__policy}{hash\+\_\+standard\+\_\+resize\+\_\+policy}, using \doxylink{class____gnu__pbds_1_1hash__exponential__size__policy}{hash\+\_\+exponential\+\_\+size\+\_\+policy} and \doxylink{class____gnu__pbds_1_1hash__load__check__resize__trigger}{hash\+\_\+load\+\_\+check\+\_\+resize\+\_\+trigger}.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyTemplParams}
